	pipil = {
		graphical_cultures = { mesonativegfx mesoamericangfx mongolgfx muslimgfx }
		color = { 0.85 0.48 0.07 }
		
		horde = yes
		
		used_for_random = no
		
	male_names = {
			Eztli Ichtaca Icnoyotl Ihuicatl Itotia Ixtli Izel Mazatl M
			eztli Nahuatl Tenoch Toltecatl Zuma    
		
			Acalan Acacitli Acamapichtli Acolmiztli Aculnahuacatl Ahuiliztli 
			Ahuitzotl Atl Axayacatl Cacamatzin Chimalli Chimalpilli Chimalpopoca 
			Cipac Coanacoch Coatl Cozahtli Cuauhtemoc Cuauhtl Cuetlachtli Cuetzpalli Cuixtli Cuitlahuac 
			Huitzilin Huitzilihuitl Huitzitl Huitztecol Iquehuacatzin Itzcoatl 
			Itzli Itzcuintli Ixtlilxochitl Mahchimaleh Matlal Mazatl Matlalihuitl Matlatzincatzin Maxtla Miztli Moctezuma Moquihuix Necuametl Nezahualcoyotl Nezahualpilli Nochehuatl 
			Ocuil Olli Opochtli Ozomatli Quauhtli Tapayaxi Tecocoltzin Tecolotl 
			Tetlepanquetzaltzin Tezozomoc Tizoc Tizocic Tlacaelel Tlacaeleltzin 
			Tlalli Tlaloc Tochtli Tototl Tzompantzin Tlilpotonqui Topiltzin
			Totoquihuaztli Ueman Yaotl Yayauhqui Yolotli Yolyamanitzin 
			Xicohtencatl Xiuhpilli Xihuitl Xipil Xipilli Xochitl Xochipepe 
			Xochipilli Zipactonal Zolin Chicahua Coatl Ilhicamina 
			Mictlantecuhtli Ohtli Tlanextli Xiuhcoatl Yaotl 
			Omakatl Tekwehtlasa Itskwin Xochikemitl Yakika Kenmachok Tewkatl
			Kwakwaw Pantli Wewetl Ahkotlewak Temilo Tekoka Yakin Tlahtlasalok
			Quauhtemoc Potonki Pahkowatl Olopatzikatl Mimich Siwakowalt Nakyitl
			Tochwa Solin Piwiyol Nawyotl Tenikaweweh Mihto Axolin Axolotl
			Kiachton Kwawtlapochin Tlakwiton Ekaton Nochwetl Wewetekatl Ilkawalok
			Chichiton Tenochtli Telpochtli Tikoknawakatl Wekamekatl Tlilli Tetzawitl
			Itzkotokatl Popokatl Motolinia Kwilol Chichatlapal Tetepon Mekaweweh 
			Misyaotl Xiwkoskatl Akatlo Ollakatl Chikwnawakatl Welitl Elotl Witznawatl
			Sacawewe Chimalpepechtli Ahkopan Teskakowakatl Tokwal Kaltekatl 
			Tlilkemitl Tepeyakanki Chalmekatl Tlillanwewe Milli Posonki Xochiwa
			Mexicatl Tekwtlamakaski Molotekatl Tlailotlak Yaotlwewe Koyolton 
			Tekokol Tlakateotl Kwima Tlakatekpanekatl Nekwametl Yaonemitl
			Tenawak Akwawitl Tlapayaw Xochiteotl Tlowi Molotl Quennel Wetl
			Tematl Siwatekpanekatl Chatl Itsmalli Tsiwkowatl Epkowatl Cozauh
			Xolotecatl Tenan Koyotl Xochinawal Siwapan Chikotl Ihhuitl Tonal Mamas
			Masewki Amistlatoh Sekwistli Tekitl Tonekokal Mixkowatl Ekatl Kwaktlistak
			Chalchiwitl Tlahtolli Kwawitl Ahkol Tlawiskal Xelwan Nenkawitl Itzmikistli
			Yopikatl Tosmakwe Toskwekwexkatl Makwilwewe Tetlakatl Tolnawakatl Mixkoatlailotlak
			Anawakatl Sipaktli Mikistli Pankos Osomahtli Nawalkiski Matlalakatl Kiyawitl
			
		}
		female_names = {
			Cualli Ichtaca Icnoyotl Ihuicatl Ixtli Izel Mazatl Meztli 
			Nahuatl Tenoch Yolotli Zuma     
		
			Achcauhtli Acxocueitl Ahuiliztli Amoxtli Atl Atotoztli Ayauhcihuatl
			Azcalxochitzin Centehua Cihuaton Chalchiuitl Chicahua 
			Chichimecacihuatzin Chipahua Chicomecoatl Chimalma Citlali 
			Citlalli Citlalmina Coaxoch Coszcatl Cozamalotl Cuicatl Eleuia 
			Eloxochitl Etalpalli Eztli Huehue-Zaca Itotia Iuitl Ixcatzin Izel
			Malinalxochitl Manauia Matlalatzin Mecatl Meztli Miahuaxiuitl 
			Miyaoaxochitl Mizquixahual Momoztli Nahuatl Necahual Nelli Ohtli 
			Papa Patli Quiauhxochitl Sacnite Techichpotzin Tezozomoc 
			Tziquetzalpoztectzin Teiuc Teicuih Teyacapan Tepin Tezcatlan 
			Tlacotl Tlahco Tlahcoehua Toltecatl Tonalnan Tlazozomizqui
			Yoltzin Xilonen Xiloxoch Xiuhtomiyauhtzin Xochitl Xocoh Xocoyotl 
			Yaretzi Zeltzin Zyanya Atzi Chiconahui Citlalic Coaxoch Metztli 
			Nenetl Quetzal Quetzalli Tayanna Tonalnan Xitllali Zaniyah 
			Xokoyotl Xochiatlapal Kokolilok Ichpochton Yaoxochitl Okoxochitl
			Tekapan Teyauh Teyawtl Ilwikasiwatl Teichpoch Tematlalewa Sentewa
			Teikwton Mosel Xilotl Koscamichiwtekatl Tlahkoewa Mawkaxochitl Siwakokoxki
			Papanton Tlahkoton Sesiwatl Siwaton Tepiton Siwanen Chopiton
		}
		
		#from_dynasty_prefix = "of "
		founder_named_dynasties = yes
		horde = yes
		dukes_called_kings = yes
		# Chance of male children being named after their paternal or maternal grandfather, or their father. Sum must not exceed 100.
		pat_grf_name_chance = 50
		mat_grf_name_chance = 0
		father_name_chance = 0
		
		# Chance of female children being named after their paternal or maternal grandmother, or their mother. Sum must not exceed 100.
		pat_grm_name_chance = 25
		mat_grm_name_chance = 25
		mother_name_chance = 0

		allow_looting = yes

		modifier = default_culture_modifier
	}

	male_names = {
			Eztli Ichtaca Icnoyotl Ihuicatl Itotia Ixtli Izel Mazatl M
			eztli Nahuatl Tenoch Toltecatl Zuma    
		
			Acalan Acacitli Acamapichtli Acolmiztli Aculnahuacatl Ahuiliztli 
			Ahuitzotl Atl Axayacatl Cacamatzin Chimalli Chimalpilli Chimalpopoca 
			Cipac Coanacoch Coatl Cozahtli Cuauhtemoc Cuauhtl Cuetlachtli Cuetzpalli Cuixtli Cuitlahuac 
			Huitzilin Huitzilihuitl Huitzitl Huitztecol Iquehuacatzin Itzcoatl 
			Itzli Itzcuintli Ixtlilxochitl Mahchimaleh Matlal Mazatl Matlalihuitl Matlatzincatzin Maxtla Miztli Moctezuma Moquihuix Necuametl Nezahualcoyotl Nezahualpilli Nochehuatl 
			Ocuil Olli Opochtli Ozomatli Quauhtli Tapayaxi Tecocoltzin Tecolotl 
			Tetlepanquetzaltzin Tezozomoc Tizoc Tizocic Tlacaelel Tlacaeleltzin 
			Tlalli Tlaloc Tochtli Tototl Tzompantzin Tlilpotonqui Topiltzin
			Totoquihuaztli Ueman Yaotl Yayauhqui Yolotli Yolyamanitzin 
			Xicohtencatl Xiuhpilli Xihuitl Xipil Xipilli Xochitl Xochipepe 
			Xochipilli Zipactonal Zolin Chicahua Coatl Ilhicamina 
			Mictlantecuhtli Ohtli Tlanextli Xiuhcoatl Yaotl 
			Omakatl Tekwehtlasa Itskwin Xochikemitl Yakika Kenmachok Tewkatl
			Kwakwaw Pantli Wewetl Ahkotlewak Temilo Tekoka Yakin Tlahtlasalok
			Quauhtemoc Potonki Pahkowatl Olopatzikatl Mimich Siwakowalt Nakyitl
			Tochwa Solin Piwiyol Nawyotl Tenikaweweh Mihto Axolin Axolotl
			Kiachton Kwawtlapochin Tlakwiton Ekaton Nochwetl Wewetekatl Ilkawalok
			Chichiton Tenochtli Telpochtli Tikoknawakatl Wekamekatl Tlilli Tetzawitl
			Itzkotokatl Popokatl Motolinia Kwilol Chichatlapal Tetepon Mekaweweh 
			Misyaotl Xiwkoskatl Akatlo Ollakatl Chikwnawakatl Welitl Elotl Witznawatl
			Sacawewe Chimalpepechtli Ahkopan Teskakowakatl Tokwal Kaltekatl 
			Tlilkemitl Tepeyakanki Chalmekatl Tlillanwewe Milli Posonki Xochiwa
			Mexicatl Tekwtlamakaski Molotekatl Tlailotlak Yaotlwewe Koyolton 
			Tekokol Tlakateotl Kwima Tlakatekpanekatl Nekwametl Yaonemitl
			Tenawak Akwawitl Tlapayaw Xochiteotl Tlowi Molotl Quennel Wetl
			Tematl Siwatekpanekatl Chatl Itsmalli Tsiwkowatl Epkowatl Cozauh
			Xolotecatl Tenan Koyotl Xochinawal Siwapan Chikotl Ihhuitl Tonal Mamas
			Masewki Amistlatoh Sekwistli Tekitl Tonekokal Mixkowatl Ekatl Kwaktlistak
			Chalchiwitl Tlahtolli Kwawitl Ahkol Tlawiskal Xelwan Nenkawitl Itzmikistli
			Yopikatl Tosmakwe Toskwekwexkatl Makwilwewe Tetlakatl Tolnawakatl Mixkoatlailotlak
			Anawakatl Sipaktli Mikistli Pankos Osomahtli Nawalkiski Matlalakatl Kiyawitl
			
		}
		female_names = {
			Cualli Ichtaca Icnoyotl Ihuicatl Ixtli Izel Mazatl Meztli 
			Nahuatl Tenoch Yolotli Zuma     
		
			Achcauhtli Acxocueitl Ahuiliztli Amoxtli Atl Atotoztli Ayauhcihuatl
			Azcalxochitzin Centehua Cihuaton Chalchiuitl Chicahua 
			Chichimecacihuatzin Chipahua Chicomecoatl Chimalma Citlali 
			Citlalli Citlalmina Coaxoch Coszcatl Cozamalotl Cuicatl Eleuia 
			Eloxochitl Etalpalli Eztli Huehue-Zaca Itotia Iuitl Ixcatzin Izel
			Malinalxochitl Manauia Matlalatzin Mecatl Meztli Miahuaxiuitl 
			Miyaoaxochitl Mizquixahual Momoztli Nahuatl Necahual Nelli Ohtli 
			Papa Patli Quiauhxochitl Sacnite Techichpotzin Tezozomoc 
			Tziquetzalpoztectzin Teiuc Teicuih Teyacapan Tepin Tezcatlan 
			Tlacotl Tlahco Tlahcoehua Toltecatl Tonalnan Tlazozomizqui
			Yoltzin Xilonen Xiloxoch Xiuhtomiyauhtzin Xochitl Xocoh Xocoyotl 
			Yaretzi Zeltzin Zyanya Atzi Chiconahui Citlalic Coaxoch Metztli 
			Nenetl Quetzal Quetzalli Tayanna Tonalnan Xitllali Zaniyah 
			Xokoyotl Xochiatlapal Kokolilok Ichpochton Yaoxochitl Okoxochitl
			Tekapan Teyauh Teyawtl Ilwikasiwatl Teichpoch Tematlalewa Sentewa
			Teikwton Mosel Xilotl Koscamichiwtekatl Tlahkoewa Mawkaxochitl Siwakokoxki
			Papanton Tlahkoton Sesiwatl Siwaton Tepiton Siwanen Chopiton
		}
		
		#from_dynasty_prefix = "of "
		founder_named_dynasties = yes
		dukes_called_kings = yes
		# Chance of male children being named after their paternal or maternal grandfather, or their father. Sum must not exceed 100.
		pat_grf_name_chance = 50
		mat_grf_name_chance = 0
		father_name_chance = 0
		
		# Chance of female children being named after their paternal or maternal grandmother, or their mother. Sum must not exceed 100.
		pat_grm_name_chance = 25
		mat_grm_name_chance = 25
		mother_name_chance = 0

		allow_looting = yes

		modifier = default_culture_modifier
	}
